\item üêû Bugfixes
\end{DoxyItemize}

\item üìö Documentation improvements
\item üåç Improve Spanish, Portuguese, Chinese locales on the Data Grid component.
\item üåç Improve Dutch locale on the Date and Time Picker components.
\item üêû Bugfixes
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\itshape Oct 4, 2024}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 26 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üîÅ Automatic parents and children selection for Data Grid \href{https://mui.com/x/react-data-grid/tree-data/}{\texttt{ "{}tree data"{}}} and \href{https://mui.com/x/react-data-grid/row-grouping/}{\texttt{ "{}row grouping"{}}} features
\item üí´ Support {\ttfamily min\+Height} and {\ttfamily max\+Height} on flex parent container for the Data Grid component
\item üéÅ Export {\ttfamily public\+API} from the {\ttfamily use\+Tree\+Item2\+Utils} hook for the Tree View
\item üåç Improve Bulgarian (bg-\/\+BG), Croatian (hr-\/\+HR), French (fr-\/\+FR), German (de-\/\+DE), Japanese (ja-\/\+JP) and Vietnamese (vi-\/\+VN) locales and add Portuguese (pt-\/\+PT) locale on the Data Grid component
\item üåè Improve Czech (cs-\/\+CZ) and Portuguese (pt-\/\+BR) locales and add Bulgarian (bg-\/\+BG), Croatian (hr-\/\+HR) and Portuguese (pt-\/\+PT) locales on the Pickers components
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\itshape Aug 1, 2024}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2520}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{üíµ Our commercial offering is evolving}{üíµ Our commercial offering is evolving}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2520}
The \href{https://mui.com/x/introduction/licensing/\#pro-plan}{\texttt{ Pro plan}} is receiving two new packages\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/tree-\/view-\/pro} (available today!)
\item {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/charts-\/pro} (available in the coming weeks)
\end{DoxyItemize}

As always, every feature released as part of the MIT plan will remain free and MIT licensed forever.

This expansion of the Pro plan comes with some adjustments to our pricing strategy. Learn more about those in the \href{https://mui.com/blog/mui-x-sep-2024-price-update/}{\texttt{ Upcoming changes to MUI¬†X pricing in 2024}} blog post.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2521}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Highlights}{Highlights}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2521}
We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 12 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üéÅ Introduce \href{https://mui.com/x/react-tree-view/rich-tree-view/ordering/}{\texttt{ item reordering using drag and drop}} on the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Rich\+Tree\+View\+Pro /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component


\item üì¶ Support Common\+JS bundle out of the box on {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/charts} by adding vendored D3 dependencies.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This modifies how the package imports D3.\+js. It will impact you if you use {\ttfamily d3} packages installed by {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/charts} and don\textquotesingle{}t have them in your {\ttfamily package.\+json}. You shouldn\textquotesingle{}t be affected otherwise.
\item For more context, the initial issue is caused by D3 only exporting ESM.


\item The solution up until now was to export charts with only ESM. But some frameworks are confused by this configuration.


\item So in order to fix this, we are providing a CJS version of D3.


\end{DoxyItemize}
\item üåç Improve Turkish (tr-\/\+TR) locale on the Data Grid
\item üåç Improve Finnish (fi-\/\+FI) locale on the Date and Time Pickers
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2522}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2522}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 10 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üõ∞ Introduce server-\/side data source for improved server integration in the Data Grid.

Supports server-\/side pagination, sorting and filtering on plain and tree data, and automatic caching.

To enable, provide a {\ttfamily get\+Rows} function to the {\ttfamily unstable\+\_\+data\+Source} prop on the Data Grid component.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ dataSource\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ getRows:\ async\ (params:\ GridServerGetRowsParams)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ const\ data\ =\ await\ fetch(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}https://api.example.com/data?\$\{new\ URLSearchParams(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ page:\ params.page,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pageSize:\ params.pageSize,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ sortModel:\ JSON.stringify(params.sortModel),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ filterModel:\ JSON.stringify(params.filterModel),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}).toString()\}`,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ return\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ rows:\ data.rows,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ totalRows:\ data.totalRows,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{<DataGridPro}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ unstable\_dataSource=\{dataSource\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \{...otherProps\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{/>}

\end{DoxyCode}


See \href{https://mui.com/x/react-data-grid/server-side-data/}{\texttt{ server-\/side data documentation}} for more details.

\item üé® Support color scales in Charts (\#12490) @alexfauquette Add a \href{https://mui.com/x/react-charts/styling/\#values-color}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily color\+Map} configuration}} to an axis, and the chart will use it to select colors. Each impacted chart (\href{https://mui.com/x/react-charts/bars/\#color-scale}{\texttt{ bar charts}}, \href{https://mui.com/x/react-charts/lines/\#color-scale}{\texttt{ line charts}}, \href{https://mui.com/x/react-charts/scatter/\#color-scale}{\texttt{ scatter charts}}) has a dedicated section explaining how this color map is impacting it.

{\itshape Mar 22, 2024}

We\textquotesingle{}re excited to \href{https://mui.com/blog/mui-x-v7/}{\texttt{ announce the first v7 stable release}}! üéâüöÄ

This is now the officially supported major version, where we\textquotesingle{}ll keep rolling out new features, bug fixes, and improvements. Migration guides are available with a complete list of the breaking changes\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://mui.com/x/migration/migration-data-grid-v6/}{\texttt{ Data Grid}}
\item \href{https://mui.com/x/migration/migration-pickers-v6/}{\texttt{ Date and Time Pickers}}
\item \href{https://mui.com/x/migration/migration-tree-view-v6/}{\texttt{ Tree View}}
\item \href{https://mui.com/x/migration/migration-charts-v6/}{\texttt{ Charts}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 12 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üöÄ Improve the usage of custom {\ttfamily view\+Renderers} on {\ttfamily Date\+Time\+Picker} (\#12441) @\+Lukas\+Ty
\item ‚ú® Set focus on the focused Tree Item instead of the Tree View (\#12226) @flaviendelangle
\item üïπÔ∏è Support controlled {\ttfamily density} for the Data Grid (\#12332) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item üéÅ Dynamic virtualization range for the Data Grid (\#12353) @romgrk
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2785}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2785}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2786}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2786}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily density} is a \href{https://mui.com/x/react-data-grid/accessibility/\#set-the-density-programmatically}{\texttt{ controlled prop}} now, if you were previously passing the {\ttfamily density} prop to the Data Grid, you will need to do one of the following\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Move it to the {\ttfamily initial\+State.\+density} to initialize it.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DataGrid}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ density="{}compact"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ initialState=\{\{\ density:\ "{}compact"{}\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Move it to the state and use {\ttfamily on\+Density\+Change} callback to update the {\ttfamily density} prop accordingly for it to work as expected.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ const\ [density,\ setDensity]\ =\ React.useState<GridDensity>('compact');}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DataGrid}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ density="{}compact"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ density=\{density\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ onDensityChange=\{(newDensity)\ =>\ setDensity(newDensity)\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The selector {\ttfamily grid\+Density\+Value\+Selector} was removed, use the {\ttfamily grid\+Density\+Selector} instead.
\item The props {\ttfamily row\+Buffer} and {\ttfamily column\+Buffer} were renamed to {\ttfamily row\+Buffer\+Px} and {\ttfamily column\+Buffer\+Px}. Their value is now a pixel value rather than a number of items. Their default value is now {\ttfamily 150}.
\item The props {\ttfamily row\+Threshold} and {\ttfamily column\+Threshold} have been removed. If you had the {\ttfamily row\+Threshold} prop set to {\ttfamily 0} to force new rows to be rendered more often ‚Äì this is no longer necessary.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2787}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2787}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Allow to control the grid density (\#12332) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Dynamic virtualization range (\#12353) @romgrk
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Fix {\ttfamily Element\+Type} usage (\#12479) @cherniavskii
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Fix cell value formatting on copy (\#12357) @sai6855
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Fix checkbox selection is keeping selection when filtering (\#11751) @g1mishra
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Make {\ttfamily rows} an optional prop (\#12478) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2788}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2788}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2789}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2789}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0}, plus\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Add support for confirmation before clipboard paste (\#12225) @cherniavskii
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Fix single grouping column sorting (\#9679) @cherniavskii
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Fix boolean cell not rendered in group rows (\#12492) @sai6855
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2790}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Date and Time Pickers}{Date and Time Pickers}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2790}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2791}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2791}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily Desktop\+Date\+Time\+Picker} view rendering has been optimized by using the same technique as for {\ttfamily Desktop\+Date\+Time\+Range\+Picker}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily date\+Time\+View\+Renderers} have been removed in favor of reusing existing time view renderers ({\ttfamily render\+Time\+View\+Clock}, {\ttfamily render\+Digital\+Clock\+Time\+View} and {\ttfamily render\+Multi\+Section\+Digital\+Clock\+Time\+View}) and date view renderer ({\ttfamily render\+Date\+View\+Calendar}).
\item Passing {\ttfamily render\+Time\+View\+Clock} to time view renderers will no longer revert to the old behavior of rendering only date or time view.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2792}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2792}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}fields\mbox{]} Allow to override the separator between the start and the end date in all range fields (\#12174) @flaviendelangle

\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2797}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2797}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The required {\ttfamily node\+Id} prop used by {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Tree\+Item /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} has been renamed to {\ttfamily item\+Id} for consistency\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <TreeView>}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ <TreeItem\ label="{}Item\ 1"{}\ nodeId="{}one"{}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ <TreeItem\ label="{}Item\ 1"{}\ itemId="{}one"{}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ </TreeView>}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The focus is now applied to the Tree Item root element instead of the Tree View root element.

This change will allow new features that require the focus to be on the Tree Item, like the drag and drop reordering of items. It also solves several issues with focus management, like the inability to scroll to the focused item when a lot of items are rendered.

This will mostly impact how you write tests to interact with the Tree View\+:

For example, if you were writing a test with {\ttfamily react-\/testing-\/library}, here is what the changes could look like\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ it('test\ example\ on\ first\ item',\ ()\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ const\ \{\ getByRole\ \}\ =\ render(}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ const\ \{\ getAllByRole\ \}\ =\ render(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ <SimpleTreeView>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <TreeItem\ nodeId="{}one"{}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ <TreeItem\ nodeId="{}two"{}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ </SimpleTreeView>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ const\ tree\ =\ getByRole('tree');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ const\ firstTreeItem\ =\ getAllByRole('treeitem')[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ act(()\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ tree.focus();}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ firstTreeItem.focus();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ fireEvent.keyDown(tree,\ \{\ key:\ 'ArrowDown'\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ fireEvent.keyDown(firstTreeItem,\ \{\ key:\ 'ArrowDown'\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \})}

\end{DoxyCode}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 11 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ü¶• The Lazy loading feature is now stable and the {\ttfamily lazy\+Loading} feature flag was removed from the {\ttfamily experimental\+Features} prop.
\item üåç Improve Japanese (ja-\/\+JP) locale for the Data Grid
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2803}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2803}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2804}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2804}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily column\+Header-\/-\/show\+Column\+Border} class was replaced by {\ttfamily column\+Header-\/-\/with\+Left\+Border} and {\ttfamily column\+Header-\/-\/with\+Right\+Border}.
\item The {\ttfamily column\+Headers\+Inner}, {\ttfamily column\+Headers\+Inner-\/-\/scrollable}, and {\ttfamily column\+Header\+Drop\+Zone} classes were removed since the inner wrapper was removed in our effort to simplify the DOM structure and improve accessibility.
\item The {\ttfamily pinned\+Column\+Headers}, {\ttfamily pinned\+Column\+Headers-\/-\/left}, and {\ttfamily pinned\+Column\+Headers-\/-\/right} classes were removed along with the element they were applied to. The pinned column headers now use `position\+: \textquotesingle{}sticky'\`{} and are rendered in the same row element as the regular column headers.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2805}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+7}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+7}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2805}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The component used to animate the item children is now defined as a slot on the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Tree\+Item /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component.

If you were passing a {\ttfamily Transition\+Component} or {\ttfamily Transition\+Props} to your {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Tree\+Item /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component, you need to use the new {\ttfamily group\+Transition} slot on this component\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <SimpleTreeView>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ <TreeItem}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ nodeId="{}1"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ label="{}Node\ 1"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ \ TransitionComponent=\{Fade\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ slots=\{\{\ groupTransition:\ Fade\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ \ TransitionProps=\{\{\ timeout:\ 600\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ slotProps=\{\{\ groupTransition:\ \{\ timeout:\ 600\ \}\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ </SimpleTreeView>}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily group} class of the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Tree\+Item /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component has been renamed to {\ttfamily group\+Transition} to match with its new slot name.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ StyledTreeItem\ =\ styled(TreeItem)(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ [`\&\ .\$\{treeItemClasses.group\}`]:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ [`\&\ .\$\{treeItemClasses.groupTransition\}`]:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ marginLeft:\ 20,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \});}

\end{DoxyCode}

Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+4}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2849}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Date and Time Pickers}{Date and Time Pickers}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2849}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2850}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2850}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily selected\+Sections} prop no longer accepts start and end indexes. When selecting several ‚Äî but not all ‚Äî sections, the field components were not behaving correctly, you can now only select one or all sections\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DateField}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ selectedSections=\{\{\ startIndex:\ 0,\ endIndex:\ 0\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ selectedSections=\{0\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ //\ If\ the\ field\ has\ 3\ sections}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ selectedSections=\{\{\ startIndex:\ 0,\ endIndex:\ 2\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ selectedSections="{}all"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The headless field hooks (e.\+g.\+: {\ttfamily use\+Date\+Field}) now returns a new prop called {\ttfamily enable\+Accessible\+Field\+DOMStructure}. This property is utilized to determine whether the anticipated UI is constructed using an accessible DOM structure. Learn more about this new \href{/x/react-date-pickers/fields/\#accessible-dom-structure}{\texttt{ accessible DOM structure}}.

When building a custom UI, you are most-\/likely only supporting one DOM structure, so you can remove {\ttfamily enable\+Accessible\+Field\+DOMStructure} before it is passed to the DOM\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ function\ MyCustomTextField(props)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ const\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ //\ Should\ be\ ignored}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ enableAccessibleFieldDOMStructure,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ ...\ rest\ of\ the\ props\ you\ are\ using}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}\ =\ props;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ return\ (\ /*\ Some\ UI\ to\ edit\ the\ date\ */\ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ function\ MyCustomField(props)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useDateField<Dayjs,\ false,\ typeof\ textFieldProps>(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ ...props,}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ //\ If\ you\ only\ support\ one\ DOM\ structure,\ we\ advise\ you\ to\ hardcode\ it\ here\ to\ avoid\ unwanted\ switches\ in\ your\ application}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ enableAccessibleFieldDOMStructure:\ false,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ return\ <MyCustomTextField\ ref=\{ref\}\ \{...fieldResponse\}\ />;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ function\ App()\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ return\ <DatePicker\ slots=\{\{\ field:\ MyCustomField\ \}\}\ />;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The following internal types were exported by mistake and have been removed from the public API\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Use\+Date\+Field\+Defaultized\+Props}
\item {\ttfamily Use\+Time\+Field\+Defaultized\+Props}
\item {\ttfamily Use\+Date\+Time\+Field\+Defaultized\+Props}
\item {\ttfamily Use\+Single\+Input\+Date\+Range\+Field\+Component\+Props}
\item {\ttfamily Use\+Single\+Input\+Time\+Range\+Field\+Component\+Props}
\item {\ttfamily Use\+Single\+Input\+Date\+Time\+Range\+Field\+Component\+Props}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2851}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+4}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+4}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2851}

{\itshape Feb 1, 2024}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 12 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üèÉ Improve the filtering performance of the Data Grid by changing the {\ttfamily Grid\+Col\+Def} methods signatures (\#11573) @cherniavskii
\item üéÅ The Line Chart component now has animation by default (\#11620) @alexfauquette
\item üöÄ All charts have click handlers (\#11411) @alexfauquette Test their respective documentation demonstrations to know more about the data format\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-charts/scatter/\#click-event}{\texttt{ Scatter Chart}}
\item \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-charts/lines/\#click-event}{\texttt{ Line Chart}}
\item \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-charts/bars/\#click-event}{\texttt{ Bar Chart}}
\item \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-charts/pie/\#click-event}{\texttt{ Pie Chart}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Big thanks to @giladappsforce and @yaredtsy for their contribution on exploring this feature.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2884}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2884}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2885}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2885}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}value\+Getter'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ valueGetter:\ (\{\ value,\ row\ \})\ =>\ value,}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ valueGetter:\ (value,\ row,\ column,\ apiRef)\ =>\ value,}

\end{DoxyCode}


The {\ttfamily Grid\+Value\+Getter\+Params} interface has been removed\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ const\ customValueGetter\ =\ (params:\ GridValueGetterParams)\ =>\ params.row.budget;}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ const\ customValueGetter:\ GridValueGetterFn\ =\ (value,\ row)\ =>\ row.budget;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}value\+Formatter'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ valueFormatter:\ (\{\ value\ \})\ =>\ value,}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ valueFormatter:\ (value,\ row,\ column,\ apiRef)\ =>\ value,}

\end{DoxyCode}


The {\ttfamily Grid\+Value\+Formatter\+Params} interface has been removed\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ const\ gridDateFormatter\ =\ (\{\ value,\ field,\ id\ \}:\ GridValueFormatterParams<Date>)\ =>\ value.toLocaleDateString();}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ const\ gridDateFormatter:\ GridValueFormatter\ =\ (value:\ Date)\ =>\ value.toLocaleDateString();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}value\+Setter'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ valueSetter:\ (params)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ const\ [firstName,\ lastName]\ =\ params.value!.toString().split('\ ');}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ return\ \{\ ...params.row,\ firstName,\ lastName\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ valueSetter:\ (value,\ row)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ const\ [firstName,\ lastName]\ =\ value!.toString().split('\ ');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ return\ \{\ ...row,\ firstName,\ lastName\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The {\ttfamily Grid\+Value\+Setter\+Params} interface has been removed\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ const\ setFullName\ =\ (params:\ GridValueSetterParams)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ const\ [firstName,\ lastName]\ =\ params.value!.toString().split('\ ');}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ return\ \{\ ...params.row,\ firstName,\ lastName\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ const\ setFullName:\ GridValueSetter<Row>\ =\ (value,\ row)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ const\ [firstName,\ lastName]\ =\ value!.toString().split('\ ');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ return\ \{\ ...row,\ firstName,\ lastName\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}value\+Parser'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ valueParser:\ (value,\ params:\ GridCellParams)\ =>\ value.toLowerCase(),}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ valueParser:\ (value,\ row,\ column,\ apiRef)\ =>\ value.toLowerCase(),}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}col\+Span'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ colSpan:\ (\{\ row,\ field,\ value\ \}:\ GridCellParams)\ =>\ (row.id\ ===\ 'total'\ ?\ 2\ :\ 1),}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ colSpan:\ (value,\ row,\ column,\ apiRef)\ =>\ (row.id\ ===\ 'total'\ ?\ 2\ :\ 1),}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}pasted\+Value\+Parser'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ pastedValueParser:\ (value,\ params)\ =>\ new\ Date(value),}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ pastedValueParser:\ (value,\ row,\ column,\ apiRef)\ =>\ new\ Date(value),}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The signature of `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}grouping\+Value\+Getter'\mbox{]}\`{} has been changed for performance reasons\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ groupingValueGetter:\ (params)\ =>\ params.value.name,}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ groupingValueGetter:\ (value:\ \{\ name:\ string\ \})\ =>\ value.name,}

\end{DoxyCode}

{\itshape Jan 26, 2024}

We are glad to announce MUI¬†X v7 beta! This version has several improvements, bug fixes, and exciting features üéâ. We want to offer a big thanks to the 7 contributors who made this release possible ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üöÄ Release the \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-date-pickers/date-time-range-picker/}{\texttt{ Date Time Range Picker}} component (\#9528) @\+Lukas\+Ty


\item üéÅ New column management panel design for the Data Grid (\#11770) @\+MBilal\+Shafi


\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2897}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2897}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2898}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2898}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The columns management component has been redesigned and the component was extracted from the {\ttfamily Columns\+Panel} which now only serves as a wrapper to display the component above the headers as a panel. As a result, a new slot {\ttfamily columns\+Management} and the related prop {\ttfamily slot\+Props.\+columns\+Management} have been introduced. The props corresponding to the columns management component which were previously passed to the prop {\ttfamily slot\+Props.\+columns\+Panel} should now be passed to {\ttfamily slot\+Props.\+columns\+Management}. {\ttfamily slot\+Props.\+columns\+Panel} could still be used to override props corresponding to the {\ttfamily Panel} component used in {\ttfamily Columns\+Panel} which uses \href{https://next.mui.com/material-ui/react-popper/}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Popper}}} component under the hood.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DataGrid}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ slotProps=\{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ columnsPanel:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ columnsManagement:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ sort:\ 'asc',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ autoFocusSearchField:\ false,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item {\ttfamily Show all} and {\ttfamily Hide all} buttons in the {\ttfamily Columns\+Panel} have been combined into one {\ttfamily Show/\+Hide All} toggle in the new columns management component. The related props {\ttfamily disable\+Show\+All\+Button} and {\ttfamily disable\+Hide\+All\+Button} have been replaced with a new prop {\ttfamily disable\+Show\+Hide\+Toggle}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DataGrid}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ disableShowAllButton}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ disableHideAllButton}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ disableShowHideToggle}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

{\itshape Jan 19, 2024}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 11 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üéÅ The Data Grid headers have been refactored to bring immense improvements to scrolling, state management, and overall performance of the grid.
\item ‚öôÔ∏è The Data Grid disabled column-\/specific features like filtering, sorting, grouping, etc. could now be accessed programmatically. See the related \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-data-grid/api-object/\#access-the-disabled-column-features}{\texttt{ docs}} section.
\item üöÄ Uplift the Simple Tree View customization examples (\#11424) @noraleonte
\item üåç Add Croatian (hr-\/\+HR), Portuguese (pt-\/\+PT), and Chinese (Hong Kong) (zh-\/\+HK) locales (\#11668) on the Data Grid @\+BCaspari
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üíî Bump {\ttfamily @mui/material} peer dependency for all packages (\#11692) @\+Lukas\+Ty The minimum required version of {\ttfamily @mui/material} is now {\ttfamily 5.\+15.\+0}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2909}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2909}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2910}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2910}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily aria\+V7} experimental flag has been removed and the Data Grid now uses the improved accessibility implementation by default. If you were using the {\ttfamily aria\+V7} flag, you can remove it from the {\ttfamily experimental\+Features} prop\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/<DataGrid\ experimentalFeatures=\{\{\ ariaV7:\ true\ \}\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{+<DataGrid\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}


The most notable changes that might affect your application or tests are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily role="{}grid"{}} attribute along with related ARIA attributes are now applied to the inner {\ttfamily div} element instead of the root {\ttfamily div} element\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/<div\ class="{}MuiDataGrid-\/root"{}\ role="{}grid"{}\ aria-\/colcount="{}5"{}\ aria-\/rowcount="{}101"{}\ aria-\/multiselectable="{}false"{}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{+<div\ class="{}MuiDataGrid-\/root"{}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ <div\ class="{}MuiDataGrid-\/toolbarContainer"{}></div>}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ <div\ class="{}MuiDataGrid-\/main"{}></div>}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ <div\ class="{}MuiDataGrid-\/main"{}\ role="{}grid"{}\ aria-\/colcount="{}5"{}\ aria-\/rowcount="{}101"{}\ aria-\/multiselectable="{}false"{}></div>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ <div\ class="{}MuiDataGrid-\/footerContainer"{}></div>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ </div>}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item When the \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-data-grid/tree-data/}{\texttt{ Tree data}} feature is used, the grid role is now {\ttfamily role="{}treegrid"{}} instead of {\ttfamily role="{}grid"{}}.
\item The Data Grid cells now have {\ttfamily role="{}gridcell"{}} instead of {\ttfamily role="{}cell"{}}.
\item The buttons in toolbar composable components {\ttfamily Grid\+Toolbar\+Columns\+Button}, {\ttfamily Grid\+Toolbar\+Filter\+Button}, {\ttfamily Grid\+Toolbar\+Density}, and {\ttfamily Grid\+Toolbar\+Export} are now wrapped with a tooltip component and have a consistent interface. To override some props corresponding to the toolbar buttons or their corresponding tooltips, you can use the {\ttfamily slot\+Props} prop. Following is an example diff. See \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-data-grid/components/\#toolbar}{\texttt{ Toolbar section}} for more details.

{\ttfamily diff function Custom\+Toolbar() \{ return ( \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Grid\+Toolbar\+Container\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Grid\+Toolbar\+Columns\+Button /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Grid\+Toolbar\+Filter\+Button
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item title="{}\+Custom filter"{} // üõë This was previously forwarded to the tooltip component
\item slot\+Props=\{\{ tooltip\+: \{ title\+: \textquotesingle{}Custom filter\textquotesingle{} \} \}\} // ‚úÖ This is the correct way now /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Grid\+Toolbar\+Density\+Selector
\item variant="{}outlined"{} // üõë This was previously forwarded to the button component
\item slot\+Props=\{\{ button\+: \{ variant\+: \textquotesingle{}outlined\textquotesingle{} \} \}\} // ‚úÖ This is the correct way now /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/\+Grid\+Toolbar\+Container\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} ); \} 
\end{DoxyItemize}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Column grouping is now enabled by default. The flag {\ttfamily column\+Grouping} is no longer needed to be passed to the {\ttfamily experimental\+Features} prop to enable it.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/<DataGrid\ experimentalFeatures=\{\{\ columnGrouping:\ true\ \}\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{+<DataGrid\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The column grouping API methods {\ttfamily get\+Column\+Group\+Path} and {\ttfamily get\+All\+Group\+Details} are no longer prefixed with {\ttfamily unstable\+\_\+}.
\item The column grouping selectors {\ttfamily grid\+Focus\+Column\+Group\+Header\+Selector} and {\ttfamily grid\+Tab\+Index\+Column\+Group\+Header\+Selector} are no longer prefixed with {\ttfamily unstable\+\_\+}.
\item The disabled column specific features like {\ttfamily hiding}, {\ttfamily sorting}, {\ttfamily filtering}, {\ttfamily pinning}, {\ttfamily row grouping}, etc could now be controlled programmatically using {\ttfamily initial\+State}, respective controlled models, or the \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-data-grid/api-object/}{\texttt{ API object}}. See the related \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-data-grid/api-object/\#access-the-disabled-column-features}{\texttt{ docs}} section.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2911}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2911}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Allow to filter non-\/filterable columns programmatically (\#11538) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Allow to programmatically sort unsortable columns (\#11512) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Fix incorrect default value for {\ttfamily filter\+Model.\+logic\+Operator} (\#11673) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Make {\ttfamily column grouping} feature stable (\#11698) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Remove the {\ttfamily aria\+V7} experimental flag (\#11428) @cherniavskii
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Start the FAQ page (\#11686) @\+MBilal\+Shafi

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2912}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2912}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2913}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2913}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+9}, plus\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Allow aggregation to be applied for non-\/aggregable columns (\#11574) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Allow programmatically grouping non-\/groupable columns (\#11539) @\+MBilal\+Shafi
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2914}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Date and Time Pickers}{Date and Time Pickers}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2914}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2915}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2915}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily locales} export has been removed from the root of the packages. If you were importing locales from the root, be sure to update it\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/import\ \{\ frFR\ \}\ from\ '@mui/x-\/date-\/pickers';}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily expand\+Icon} / {\ttfamily default\+Expand\+Icon} props, used to expand the children of a node (rendered when it is collapsed), is now defined as a slot both on the Tree View and the Tree Item components.

If you were using the {\ttfamily Chevron\+Right} icon from {\ttfamily @mui/icons-\/material}, you can stop passing it to your component because it is now the default value\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/import\ ChevronRightIcon\ from\ '@mui/icons-\/material/ChevronRight';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <SimpleTreeView}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ defaultExpandIcon=\{<ChevronRightIcon\ />\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \{items\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ </SimpleTreeView>}

\end{DoxyCode}


If you were passing another icon to your Tree View component, you need to use the new {\ttfamily expand\+Icon} slot on this component\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <SimpleTreeView}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ defaultExpandIcon=\{<MyCustomExpandIcon\ />\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ slots=\{\{\ expandIcon:\ MyCustomExpandIcon\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \{items\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ </SimpleTreeView>}

\end{DoxyCode}


If you were passing another icon to your Tree Item component, you need to use the new {\ttfamily expand\+Icon} slot on this component\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ <SimpleTreeView>}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ nodeId="{}1"{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ slots=\{\{\ expandIcon:\ MyCustomExpandIcon\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ </SimpleTreeView>}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üéÅ New component to create a Tree View from a structured data source\+:

You can now directly pass your data to the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Rich\+Tree\+View /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component instead of manually converting it into JSX {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Tree\+Item /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} components\+:

{\itshape Dec 22, 2023}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 6 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üéÅ Data Grid now supports {\ttfamily Date} objects in the {\ttfamily filter\+Model}
\item üåç Improve Russian (ru-\/\+RU) locale on the Data Grid
\item üêû Bugfixes
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2951}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2951}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2952}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2952}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The filter panel no longer uses the native version of the \href{https://mui.com/material-ui/react-select/}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Select}}} component for all components.
\item The {\ttfamily get\+Option\+Value} and {\ttfamily get\+Option\+Label} props were removed from the following components\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily Grid\+Edit\+Single\+Select\+Cell}
\item {\ttfamily Grid\+Filter\+Input\+Single\+Select}
\item {\ttfamily Grid\+Filter\+Input\+Multiple\+Single\+Select}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Use the {\ttfamily get\+Option\+Value} and {\ttfamily get\+Option\+Label} properties on the {\ttfamily single\+Select} column definition instead\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ column:\ GridColDef\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ type:\ 'singleSelect',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ field:\ 'country',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ valueOptions:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \{\ code:\ 'BR',\ name:\ 'Brazil'\ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \{\ code:\ 'FR',\ name:\ 'France'\ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ getOptionValue:\ (value:\ any)\ =>\ value.code,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ getOptionLabel:\ (value:\ any)\ =>\ value.name,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily filter\+Model} now supports {\ttfamily Date} objects as values for {\ttfamily date} and {\ttfamily date\+Time} column types. The {\ttfamily filter\+Model} still accepts strings as values for {\ttfamily date} and {\ttfamily date\+Time} column types, but all updates to the {\ttfamily filter\+Model} coming from the UI (for example filter panel) will set the value as a {\ttfamily Date} object.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2953}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+6}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+6}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2953}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2954}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+6} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+6} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2954}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 9 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üí´ New recipe added for the Data Grid
\item üåç Improve Swedish (sv-\/\+SE) and Urdu (ur-\/\+PK) locales on the Data Grid
\item üêû Bugfixes
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2963}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2963}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2964}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2964}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily instance\+Id} prop is now required for state selectors. This prop is used to distinguish between multiple Data Grid instances on the same page. See \href{https://next.mui.com/x/migration/migration-data-grid-v6/\#instanceid-prop-is-required-for-state-selectors}{\texttt{ migration docs}} for more details.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2965}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2965}

Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2967}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2967}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2968}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Date and Time Pickers}{Date and Time Pickers}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2968}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2969}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2969}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The slot interfaces got renamed to match with {\ttfamily @mui/base} naming. The {\ttfamily Slots\+Component} suffix has been replaced with {\ttfamily Slots} and {\ttfamily Slots\+Components\+Props} with {\ttfamily Slot\+Props}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/DateCalendarSlotsComponent}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/DateCalendarSlotsComponentsProps}
\DoxyCodeLine{+DateCalendarSlots}
\DoxyCodeLine{+DateCalendarSlotProps}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Move {\ttfamily input\+Ref} inside the props passed to the field hooks

The field hooks now only receive the props instead of an object containing both the props and the {\ttfamily input\+Ref}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ \{\ inputRef,\ ...otherProps\ \}\ =\ props}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useDateField(\{\ props:\ otherProps,\ inputRef\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useDateField(props);}

\end{DoxyCode}


If you are using a multi input range field hook, the same applies to {\ttfamily start\+Input\+Ref} and {\ttfamily end\+Input\+Ref} params


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ \{\ inputRef:\ startInputRef,\ ...otherStartTextFieldProps\ \}\ =\ startTextFieldProps}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ \{\ inputRef:\ endInputRef,\ ...otherEndTextFieldProps\ \}\ =\ endTextFieldProps}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useMultiInputDateRangeField(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ sharedProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ startTextFieldProps:\ otherStartTextFieldProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ endTextFieldProps:\ otherEndTextFieldProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ startInputRef}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ endInputRef,}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ startTextFieldProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ endTextFieldProps}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Rename the ref returned by the field hooks to {\ttfamily input\+Ref}

When used with the v6 Text\+Field approach (where the input is an {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}input /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} HTML element), the field hooks return a ref that needs to be passed to the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}input /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} element. This ref was previously named {\ttfamily ref} and has been renamed {\ttfamily input\+Ref} for extra clarity.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useDateField(props);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/return\ <input\ ref=\{fieldResponse.ref\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{+return\ <input\ ref=\{fieldResponse.inputRef\}\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}


If you are using a multi input range field hook, the same applies to the ref in the {\ttfamily start\+Date} and {\ttfamily end\+Date} objects


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useDateField(props);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ return\ (}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ <div>}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ <input\ ref=\{fieldResponse.startDate.ref\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ <input\ ref=\{fieldResponse.startDate.inputRef\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ <span>‚Äì</span>}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ <input\ ref=\{fieldResponse.endDate.ref\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ <input\ ref=\{fieldResponse.endDate.inputRef\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ </div>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ )}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Restructure the API of {\ttfamily use\+Clearable\+Field}

The {\ttfamily use\+Clearable\+Field} hook API has been simplified to now take a {\ttfamily props} parameter instead of a {\ttfamily field\+Props}, {\ttfamily Input\+Props}, {\ttfamily clearable}, {\ttfamily on\+Clear}, {\ttfamily slots} and {\ttfamily slot\+Props} parameters.

You should now be able to directly pass the returned value from your field hook (e.\+g\+: {\ttfamily use\+Date\+Field}) to {\ttfamily use\+Clearable\+Field}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ fieldResponse\ =\ useDateField(props);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ \{\ InputProps,\ onClear,\ clearable,\ slots,\ slotProps,\ ...otherFieldProps\ \}\ =\ fieldResponse}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ \{\ InputProps:\ ProcessedInputProps,\ fieldProps:\ processedFieldProps\ \}\ =\ useClearableField(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ fieldProps:\ otherFieldProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ InputProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ clearable,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ onClear,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ slots,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ slotProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\});}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ return\ <MyCustomTextField\ \{...processedFieldProps\}\ InputProps=\{ProcessedInputProps\}\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ processedFieldProps\ =\ useClearableField(fieldResponse);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+return\ <MyCustomTextField\ \{...processedFieldProps\}\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2970}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+5}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2970}

{\itshape Dec 8, 2023}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 11 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üöÄ The scatter charts now use voronoi to trigger items

Users needed to hover the item to highlight the scatter item or show the tooltip. Now they can interact with data by triggering the closest element. See the \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-charts/scatter/\#interaction}{\texttt{ docs page}} for more info.
\item üìö Add \href{https://next.mui.com/x/react-date-pickers/faq/}{\texttt{ Pickers FAQ page}}
\item üéâ The Data Grid Header filters feature is now stable
\item üåç Improve Danish (da-\/\+DK) locale on Data Grid
\item üêû Bugfixes
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2977}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2977}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2978}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2978}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The header filters feature is now stable. {\ttfamily unstable\+\_\+} prefix is removed from prop {\ttfamily header\+Filters} and related exports. See \href{https://next.mui.com/x/migration/migration-data-grid-v6/\#filtering}{\texttt{ migration docs}} for more details.
\item The `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}type'\mbox{]}{\ttfamily has been narrowed down to only accept the built-\/in column types. Type\+Script users need to use the}Grid\+Col\+Def\`{} interface when defining columns\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ üõë\ \`{}type`\ is\ inferred\ as\ \`{}string`\ and\ is\ too\ wide}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ columns\ =\ [\{\ type:\ 'number',\ field:\ 'id'\ \}];}
\DoxyCodeLine{<DataGrid\ columns=\{columns\}\ />;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ ‚úÖ\ \`{}type`\ is\ \`{}'number'`}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ columns:\ GridColDef[]\ =\ [\{\ type:\ 'number',\ field:\ 'id'\ \}];}
\DoxyCodeLine{<DataGrid\ columns=\{columns\}\ />;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ ‚úÖ\ Alternalively,\ \`{}as\ const`\ can\ be\ used\ to\ narrow\ down\ the\ type}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ columns\ =\ [\{\ type:\ 'number'\ as\ const,\ field:\ 'id'\ \}];}
\DoxyCodeLine{<DataGrid\ columns=\{columns\}\ />;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2979}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+4}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+4}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2979}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Added a guard for reorder cells (\#11159) @michelengelen
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\mbox{]} Narrow down `Grid\+Col\+Def\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}type'\mbox{]}\`{} (\#11270) @cherniavskii
\item \mbox{[}l10n\mbox{]} Improve Danish (da-\/\+DK) locale (\#11304) @goibon
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2980}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+4} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+4} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2980}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+4}, plus\+:

{\itshape Dec 4, 2023}

We\textquotesingle{}d like to offer a big thanks to the 15 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üöÄ Support localized start of the week on pickers\textquotesingle{} {\ttfamily Adapter\+Luxon}

When using Luxon 3.\+4.\+4 or higher, the start of the week will be defined by the date locale (e.\+g.\+: Sunday for {\ttfamily en-\/\+US}, Monday for {\ttfamily fr-\/\+FR}).
\item üìà Fix a lot of Charts package issues
\item üéâ The Data Grid features Cell selection and Clipboard paste are now stable
\item üåç Improve Bulgarian (bg-\/\+BG) locale on Data Grid
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2988}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2988}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2989}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2989}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The clipboard paste feature is now enabled by default. The flag {\ttfamily clipboard\+Paste} is no longer needed to be passed to the {\ttfamily experimental\+Features} prop.
\item The clipboard related exports {\ttfamily ignore\+Value\+Formatter\+During\+Export} and {\ttfamily split\+Clipboard\+Pasted\+Text} are no longer prefixed with {\ttfamily unstable\+\_\+}.
\item The deprecated constants {\ttfamily SUBMIT\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+STROKE\+\_\+\+TIME} and {\ttfamily SUBMIT\+\_\+\+FILTER\+\_\+\+DATE\+\_\+\+STROKE\+\_\+\+TIME} have been removed from the Data Grid exports. Use the \href{https://next.mui.com/x/api/data-grid/data-grid/\#data-grid-prop-filterDebounceMs}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily filter\+Debounce\+Ms}}} prop to customize filter debounce time.
\item The {\ttfamily slots.\+preferences\+Panel} slot and the {\ttfamily slot\+Props.\+preferences\+Panel} prop were removed. Use {\ttfamily slots.\+panel} and {\ttfamily slot\+Props.\+panel} instead.
\item The {\ttfamily Grid\+Preferences\+Panel} component is not exported anymore as it wasn\textquotesingle{}t meant to be used outside of the Data Grid.
\item The {\ttfamily unstable\+\_\+} prefix has been removed from the cell selection props listed below.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+3}, plus\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Fix aggregated column ignoring column definition changes (\#11129) @cherniavskii
\item \mbox{[}Data\+Grid\+Premium\mbox{]} Make Cell selection feature stable (\#11246) @\+MBilal\+Shafi

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2993}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Date and Time Pickers}{Date and Time Pickers}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2993}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2994}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2994}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The Date and Time Pickers now use the localized week when using {\ttfamily Adapter\+Luxon} and Luxon v3.\+4.\+4 or higher is installed. This new behavior allows {\ttfamily Adapter\+Luxon} to have the same behavior as the other adapters. If you want to keep the start of the week on Monday even if your locale says otherwise, you can hardcode the week settings as follows\+: The Firefox browser currently does not support this behavior because the \href{https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Intl/Locale/getWeekInfo}{\texttt{ get\+Week\+Info}} API is not yet implemented.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ Settings,\ Info\ \}\ from\ 'luxon';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{Settings.defaultWeekSettings\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ firstDay:\ 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ minimalDays:\ Info.getMinimumDaysInFirstWeek(),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ weekend:\ [6,\ 7],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item Add new parameters to the {\ttfamily shortcuts} slot {\ttfamily on\+Change} callback

The {\ttfamily on\+Change} callback fired when selecting a shortcut now requires two new parameters (previously they were optional)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The \href{/x/react-date-pickers/shortcuts/\#behavior-when-selecting-a-shortcut}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily change\+Importance}}} of the shortcut.
\item The {\ttfamily item} containing the entire shortcut object.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ CustomShortcuts\ =\ (props)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ return\ (}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ <React.Fragment>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{props.items.map(item\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ const\ value\ =\ item.getValue(\{\ isValid:\ props.isValid\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ (}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ <button}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ onClick=\{()\ =>\ onChange(value)\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ onClick=\{()\ =>\ onChange(value,\ props.changeImportance\ ??\ 'accept',\ item)\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{value\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ </button>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ </React.Fragment>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DatePicker\ slots=\{\{\ shortcuts:\ CustomShortcuts\ \}\}\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Usage of {\ttfamily Adapter\+Dayjs} with the {\ttfamily custom\+Parse\+Format} plugin The call to {\ttfamily dayjs.\+extend(custom\+Parse\+Format\+Plugin)} has been moved to the {\ttfamily Adapter\+Dayjs} constructor. This allows users to pass custom options to this plugin before the adapter uses it.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If you are using this plugin before the rendering of the first {\ttfamily Localization\+Provider} component and did not call {\ttfamily dayjs.\+extend} in your own codebase, you will need to manually extend {\ttfamily dayjs}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ dayjs\ from\ 'dayjs';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ customParseFormatPlugin\ from\ 'dayjs/plugin/customParseFormat';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{dayjs.extend(customParseFormatPlugin);}

\end{DoxyCode}


The other plugins are still added before the adapter initialization.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2995}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+3}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+3}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2995}

\item üìà Export missing Charts props

\item üåç Add Macedonian (mk) locale and improve German (de-\/\+DE) locale on Pickers

\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3001}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3001}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3003}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-pro-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3003}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3004}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/premium@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2} \href{https://mui.com/r/x-premium-svg-link}{\texttt{ }}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3004}
Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/data-\/grid-\/pro@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3005}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Date and Time Pickers}{Date and Time Pickers}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3005}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3006}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3006}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The deprecated {\ttfamily should\+Disable\+Clock} prop has been removed in favor of the more flexible {\ttfamily should\+Disable\+Time} prop. The {\ttfamily should\+Disable\+Clock} prop received {\ttfamily value} as a {\ttfamily number} of hours, minutes, or seconds. Instead, the {\ttfamily should\+Disable\+Time} prop receives the date object (based on the used adapter).

You can read more about the deprecation of this prop in \href{https://next.mui.com//x/migration/migration-pickers-v5/\#\%E2\%9C\%85-rename-or-refactor-shoulddisabletime-prop}{\texttt{ v6 migration guide}}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DateTimePicker}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ shouldDisableClock=\{(timeValue,\ view)\ =>\ view\ ===\ 'hours'\ \&\&\ timeValue\ <\ 12\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ shouldDisableTime=\{(value,\ view)\ =>\ view\ ===\ 'hours'\ \&\&\ value.hour()\ <\ 12\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+date\+With\+Timezone} method has been removed and its content moved to the {\ttfamily date} method. You can use the {\ttfamily adapter.\+date} method instead\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ adapter.dateWithTimezone(undefined,\ 'system');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ adapter.date(undefined,\ 'system');}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily day\+Picker\+Classes} variable has been renamed to {\ttfamily day\+Calendar\+Classes} to be consistent with the new name of the {\ttfamily Day\+Calendar} component introduced in v6.\+0.\+0.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ import\ \{\ dayPickerClasses\ \}\ from\ '@mui/x-\/date-\/pickers/DateCalendar';}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ import\ \{\ dayCalendarClasses\ \}\ from\ '@mui/x-\/date-\/pickers/DateCalendar';}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The deprecated {\ttfamily default\+Calendar\+Month} prop has been removed in favor of the more flexible {\ttfamily reference\+Date} prop.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ <DateCalendar\ defaultCalendarMonth=\{dayjs('2022-\/04-\/01')\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ <DateCalendar\ referenceDate\{dayjs('2022-\/04-\/01')\}\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+date} method now has the v6 {\ttfamily adapter.\+date\+With\+Timezone} method behavior. It no longer accepts {\ttfamily any} as a value but only {\ttfamily string \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} null \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} undefined}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ adapter.date(new\ Date());}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ adapter.date();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ adapter.date(new\ Date('2022-\/04-\/17');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ adapter.date('2022-\/04-\/17');}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ adapter.date(new\ Date(2022,\ 3,\ 17,\ 4,\ 5,\ 34));}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ adapter.date('2022-\/04-\/17T04:05:34');}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ adapter.date(new\ Date('Invalid\ Date'));}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ adapter.getInvalidDate();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3007}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2}}{{\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+2}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3007}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The string argument of the {\ttfamily day\+Of\+Week\+Formatter} prop has been replaced in favor of the date object to allow more flexibility.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <DateCalendar}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ //\ If\ you\ were\ still\ using\ the\ day\ string,\ you\ can\ get\ it\ back\ with\ your\ date\ library.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ dayOfWeekFormatter=\{dayStr\ =>\ \`{}\$\{dayStr\}.`\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ dayOfWeekFormatter=\{day\ =>\ \`{}\$\{day.format('dd')\}.`\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ //\ If\ you\ were\ already\ using\ the\ day\ object,\ just\ remove\ the\ first\ argument.}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ dayOfWeekFormatter=\{(\_dayStr,\ day)\ =>\ \`{}\$\{day.format('dd')\}.`\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ dayOfWeekFormatter=\{day\ =>\ \`{}\$\{day.format('dd')\}.`\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The imports related to the {\ttfamily calendar\+Header} slot have been moved from {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers/\+Date\+Calendar} to {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers/\+PIckers\+Calendar\+Header}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ export\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ pickersCalendarHeaderClasses,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ PickersCalendarHeaderClassKey,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ PickersCalendarHeaderClasses,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ PickersCalendarHeader,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ PickersCalendarHeaderProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ PickersCalendarHeaderSlotsComponent,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ PickersCalendarHeaderSlotsComponentsProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ ExportedPickersCalendarHeaderProps,}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\}\ from\ '@mui/x-\/date-\/pickers/DateCalendar';}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\}\ from\ '@mui/x-\/date-\/pickers/PickersCalendarHeader';}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily month\+And\+Year} format has been removed. It was used in the header of the calendar views, you can replace it with the new {\ttfamily format} prop of the {\ttfamily calendar\+Header} slot\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <LocalizationProvider}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ adapter=\{AdapterDayJS\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ formats=\{\{\ monthAndYear:\ 'MM/YYYY'\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ <DatePicker}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ slotProps=\{\{\ calendarHeader:\ \{\ format:\ 'MM/YYYY'\ \}\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ <DateRangePicker}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ slotProps=\{\{\ calendarHeader:\ \{\ format:\ 'MM/YYYY'\ \}\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ />}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ <LocalizationProvider\ />}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+get\+Diff} method have been removed, you can directly use your date library\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ Day.js}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ diff\ =\ adapter.getDiff(value,\ comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ diff\ =\ value.diff(comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ Luxon}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ diff\ =\ adapter.getDiff(value,\ comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ getDiff\ =\ (value:\ DateTime,\ comparing:\ DateTime\ |\ string,\ unit?:\ AdapterUnits)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ const\ parsedComparing\ =\ typeof\ comparing\ ===\ 'string'}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ ?\ DateTime.fromJSDate(new\ Date(comparing))}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ :\ comparing;}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ if\ (unit)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ return\ Math.floor(value.diff(comparing).as(unit));}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ return\ value.diff(comparing).as('millisecond');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ diff\ =\ getDiff(value,\ comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ //\ For\ DateFns}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ diff\ =\ adapter.getDiff(value,\ comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ getDiff\ =\ (value:\ Date,\ comparing:\ Date\ |\ string,\ unit?:\ AdapterUnits)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ const\ parsedComparing\ =\ typeof\ comparing\ ===\ 'string'\ ?\ new\ Date(comparing)\ :\ comparing;}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ switch\ (unit)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'years':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInYears(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'quarters':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInQuarters(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'months':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInMonths(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'weeks':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInWeeks(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'days':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInDays(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'hours':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInHours(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'minutes':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInMinutes(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ case\ 'seconds':}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInSeconds(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ default:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ return\ dateFns.differenceInMilliseconds(value,\ parsedComparing);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ diff\ =\ getDiff(value,\ comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ Moment}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ diff\ =\ adapter.getDiff(value,\ comparing,\ unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ diff\ =\ value.diff(comparing,\ unit);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+get\+Format\+Helper\+Text} method have been removed, you can use the {\ttfamily adapter.\+expand\+Format} instead\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.getFormatHelperText(format);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.expandFormat(format);}

\end{DoxyCode}


And if you need the exact same output you can apply the following transformation\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ Day.js}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.getFormatHelperText(format);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.expandFormat(format).replace(/a/gi,\ '(a|p)m').toLocaleLowerCase();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ Luxon}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.getFormatHelperText(format);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.expandFormat(format).replace(/(a)/g,\ '(a|p)m').toLocaleLowerCase();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ DateFns}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.getFormatHelperText(format);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.expandFormat(format).replace(/(aaa|aa|a)/g,\ '(a|p)m').toLocaleLowerCase();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ For\ Moment}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.getFormatHelperText(format);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ expandedFormat\ =\ adapter.expandFormat(format).replace(/a/gi,\ '(a|p)m').toLocaleLowerCase();}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+get\+Meridiem\+Text} method have been removed, you can use the {\ttfamily adapter.\+set\+Hours}, {\ttfamily adapter.\+date} and {\ttfamily adapter.\+format} methods to recreate its behavior\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/const\ meridiem\ =\ adapter.getMeridiemText('am');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ getMeridiemText\ =\ (meridiem:\ 'am'\ |\ 'pm')\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ const\ date\ =\ adapter.setHours(adapter.date()!,\ meridiem\ ===\ 'am'\ ?\ 2\ :\ 14);}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ return\ utils.format(date,\ 'meridiem');}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ meridiem\ =\ getMeridiemText('am');}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+get\+Month\+Array} method have been removed, you can use the {\ttfamily adapter.\+start\+Of\+Year} and {\ttfamily adapter.\+add\+Months} methods to recreate its behavior\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ const\ months\ =\ [firstMonth];}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ while\ (months.length\ <\ 12)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ const\ prevMonth\ =\ months[months.length\ -\/\ 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ months.push(utils.addMonths(prevMonth,\ 1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ return\ months;}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{+}
\DoxyCodeLine{+const\ monthArray\ =\ getMonthArray(value);}

\item The {\ttfamily adapter.\+is\+Equal} method used to accept any type of value for its two input and tried to parse them before checking if they were equal.
