\item The {\ttfamily date\+Lib\+Instance} prop of {\ttfamily Localization\+Provider} does not work with {\ttfamily Adapter\+Dayjs} anymore (\#11023). This prop was used to set the pickers in UTC mode before the implementation of a proper timezone support in the components. You can learn more about the new approach on the \href{https://mui.com/x/react-date-pickers/timezone/}{\texttt{ dedicated doc page}}.

{\itshape Nov 10, 2023}

We\textquotesingle{}re thrilled to announce the first alpha release of our next major version, v7. This release introduces a few breaking changes, paving the way for the upcoming features like Pivoting and Date\+Time\+Range\+Picker.

A special shoutout to thank the 12 contributors who made this release possible. Here are some highlights ‚ú®\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item üöÄ First v7 alpha release
\item ‚ú® Fix aggregation label not showing when {\ttfamily render\+Header} is used (\#10961) @cherniavskii
\item üìò Server side data source \href{https://mui.com/x/react-data-grid/server-side-data/}{\texttt{ early documentation}}
\item üí´ New recipes added for the Data Grid
\item üìà {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Charts\+Reference\+Line /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component is now available
\item üåç Add Basque (eu) locale, improve Czech (cs-\/\+CZ) and Spanish (es-\/\+ES) locales
\item üêû Bugfixes
\item üìö Documentation improvements
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3021}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Data Grid}{Data Grid}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3021}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3022}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3022}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The deprecated {\ttfamily components} and {\ttfamily components\+Props} props have been removed. Use {\ttfamily slots} and {\ttfamily slot\+Props} instead. See \href{/x/react-data-grid/components/}{\texttt{ components section}} for more details.
\item The print export will now only print the selected rows if there are any. If there are no selected rows, it will print all rows. This makes the print export consistent with the other exports. You can \href{/x/react-data-grid/export/\#customizing-the-rows-to-export}{\texttt{ customize the rows to export by using the {\ttfamily get\+Rows\+To\+Export} function}}.
\item The {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Filter\+Fn\+V7} in {\ttfamily Grid\+Filter\+Operator} was renamed to {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Filter\+Fn}. If you use {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Filter\+Fn\+V7} directly -\/ rename it to {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Filter\+Fn}.
\item The signature of the function returned by {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Filter\+Fn} has changed for performance reasons\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ const\ getApplyFilterFn:\ GetApplyFilterFn<any,\ unknown>\ =\ (filterItem)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ if\ (!filterItem.value)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ return\ null;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ const\ filterRegex\ =\ new\ RegExp(escapeRegExp(filterItem.value),\ 'i');}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ return\ (cellParams)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ const\ \{\ value\ \}\ =\ cellParams;}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ return\ (value,\ row,\ colDef,\ apiRef)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ return\ value\ !=\ null\ ?\ filterRegex.test(String(value))\ :\ false;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Quick\+Filter\+Fn\+V7} in {\ttfamily Grid\+Col\+Def} was renamed to {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Quick\+Filter\+Fn}. If you use {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Quick\+Filter\+Fn\+V7} directly -\/ rename it to {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Quick\+Filter\+Fn}.
\item The signature of the function returned by {\ttfamily get\+Apply\+Quick\+Filter\+Fn} has changed for performance reasons\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ if\ (!value)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ return\ null;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ const\ filterRegex\ =\ new\ RegExp(escapeRegExp(value),\ 'i');}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ return\ (cellParams)\ =>\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ return\ (value,\ row,\ column,\ apiRef)\ =>\ \{}

Same changes as in {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/date-\/pickers@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+0}.\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3030}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Charts / {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/charts@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+0}}{Charts / {\ttfamily @mui/x-\/charts@7.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+0}}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3030}
\hypertarget{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3031}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md__tele-website_2node__modules_2_0dmui_2x-internals_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3031}
Types for {\ttfamily slots} and {\ttfamily slot\+Props} got renamed by removing the "{}\+Component"{} which is meaningless for charts. Unless you imported those types, to create a wrapper, you should not be impacted by this breaking change.

Here is an example of the renaming for the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Charts\+Tooltip /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/ChartsTooltipSlotsComponent}
\DoxyCodeLine{+ChartsTooltipSlots}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/ChartsTooltipSlotComponentProps}
\DoxyCodeLine{+ChartsTooltipSlotProps}

\end{DoxyCode}
